# 魔兽世界五人副本 — 饥荒风插画与角色提示词大全（HeyBro）

> **生成**：`python tools/generate_wow_famine_prompt_md.py`
> **数据**：`wowBookMonsters.json`、`wowBookBosses.json`、`reference-classic-vanilla-wow-roguelike-level-design.json`
> **副本背景图**：见下「## 通用（Dungeon backgrounds）」共 18 条 fenced 提示词（**不另建**独立副本背景 md）。可与 `wow_book_art_jobs` scene JSON 并存。
> **副本主题插画**：`### 副本主题插画` 暂缓；`wow_md_parse_jobs` 需 `include_scene` 才解析。
> **UID**：小怪 `monsterUid`（`U*`），首领 `bossUid`（`B*`）；与 `scripts/generate-wow-book-tables.mjs` 一致。
> **画风**：与 `gptimage/dont_starve_style.py` 的 `STYLE_CORE` 及下方「通用画风」块一致。
> **敌方立绘背景**：小怪为冷灰 bokeh；**全部首领**立绘均为暗红/酒红 bokeh（与 `wow_book_art_jobs` 一致）。

---

## 通用画风关键词（可粘贴到任意条目前）

> 本节以 `通用` 开头，**不会被** `wow_md_parse_jobs` 当作副本任务解析。

- **中文**：饥荒（Don't Starve）/ Klei 手绘感：墨线勾边、线宽略抖、低饱和大地色系、平涂或轻排线、木偶感比例、阴郁怪趣味。
- **English**：`Klei Don't Starve style: hand-ink outlines, slightly jittery line weight, flat or lightly hatched fills, desaturated earthy palette, puppet-like stylized proportions, subtle grim whimsy. NOT photoreal, NOT glossy anime cel, NOT soft airbrush beauty, NOT clean Pixar 3D.`
- **否定**：Avoid: circular badge UI frame, watermark, readable text, photoreal skin, glossy anime highlights, Octane 3D, busy sharp readable full dungeon map as background, gore.

### 通用｜副本背景图（补充文风，叠用在各副本背景 fenced 前后）

- **中文**：饥荒 Klei **加载画式 2D**：粗墨线、平涂或**短排线阴影**、哑色大地系；**纸片景深**（中景笔触概括，远景更淡）。熔岩/邪能等为**粉画感低饱和**、**墨线收边**，忌霓虹辉光。可极轻纸张肌理；忌 8K 写实岩石金属、忌电影体积光与镜头眩光。
- **English**：`DS/Klei loading-screen: ink outlines, flat or short-hatched shadows, desaturated earthy palette, paper-theatre depth (brushy midground, softer distance). Chalky muted lava/magic with INKED edges, NOT neon. NO volumetric god rays, NO lens flare, NO photoreal rock microdetail, NO cinematic trailer polish.`
- **否定（追加）**：Avoid: foreground mob packs or patrol squads, midground trash clusters, WoW cinematic, Hearthstone splash gloss, strong lava bloom.

---

## 通用（Dungeon backgrounds）

> 本节 `##` 标题以 `通用` 开头，`wow_md_parse_jobs` **不会**当作正式副本小节解析。下列每条 ```text``` 供**该副本一张氛围/背景图**使用（非单怪立绘）。**不另建**独立「副本背景图.md」。

### 使用说明（重要）

- **不要**在中近景画巡逻小怪、小怪群或战斗阵型；场景以**环境、地貌、光线**为主，宁可空无一人。
- **仅在远景深处**（洞口尽头/廊道消失点）留一团 **5%～8% 画面高度** 的**关底首领剪影虚影**，融入暗部：无五官可读、无肌肉特写、不做第二主体。关底首领取 `wowBookBosses.json` 中该副本 **chapterIndex 最大** 的一条。
- 画风锚点请叠用上方「## 通用画风关键词」整段。

### 怒焰裂谷（Ragefire Chasm）

```text
【副本背景图｜怒焰裂谷（Ragefire Chasm）】魔兽世界五人副本氛围场景：地下熔岩裂隙洞窟：暗红砖岩与脚浅哑色熔岩细流，热浪微微扭曲远景。 **以环境、地形与光线为主**；**中近景不出现巡逻小怪与小怪集群**（可无人物）。仅在**远景尽头/洞口深处**留一团**极淡、剪影化、融入暗部**的关底首领虚影：**巴扎兰（Bazzalan）**——约占画面高度 **5%～8%** 的斑块剪影，无面孔可读、无肌肉渲染、不成为第二视觉中心。
Klei Don't Starve loading-screen: thick hand-ink outlines, flat or lightly hatched shadows, desaturated earthy palette; **only** a tiny vague far boss silhouette at vanishing point; chalky lava/magic accents with inked edges, NO neon glow, NO volumetric god rays, NO lens flare.
Avoid: foreground mob packs, midground trash patrols, readable boss portrait, WoW cinematic trailer, photoreal rock microdetail, watermark, readable text.
```

### 斯坦索姆（Stratholme）

```text
【副本背景图｜斯坦索姆（Stratholme）】魔兽世界五人副本氛围场景：斯坦索姆废城街廊：碎裂石板、瘟疫绿雾与焦黑屋影。 **以环境、地形与光线为主**；**中近景不出现巡逻小怪与小怪集群**（可无人物）。仅在**远景尽头/洞口深处**留一团**极淡、剪影化、融入暗部**的关底首领虚影：**巴尔纳扎尔（Balnazzar）**——约占画面高度 **5%～8%** 的斑块剪影，无面孔可读、无肌肉渲染、不成为第二视觉中心。
Klei Don't Starve loading-screen: thick hand-ink outlines, flat or lightly hatched shadows, desaturated earthy palette; **only** a tiny vague far boss silhouette at vanishing point; chalky lava/magic accents with inked edges, NO neon glow, NO volumetric god rays, NO lens flare.
Avoid: foreground mob packs, midground trash patrols, readable boss portrait, WoW cinematic trailer, photoreal rock microdetail, watermark, readable text.
```


## 模板兵种（Legacy）

### 小怪与精英

#### 1. 憎恶（Abomination）
- **类型**：模板兵种
- **表 id**：`abomination`
- **monsterUid**：`U000001`

```text
【书怪小怪｜模板兵种（Legacy）】憎恶（Abomination）。魔兽世界地下城设定下的单体角色立绘或小场景胸像，方图构图、主体居中、剪影在缩略图尺度可读。 背景为高度虚化的统一冷灰 bokeh（石板灰 #94a3a8 系），低饱和、边缘略压暗炭灰 #475569，无职业色光晕、无整块抢镜彩色氛围。 Heavily blurred bokeh background dominated by unified cool neutral gray (#94a3a8, slate), low saturation, slightly darker charcoal #475569 at edges, no colored class glow. 饥荒（Don't Starve）/ Klei 手绘感：墨线勾边、线宽略抖、低饱和大地色系、平涂或轻排线、木偶感比例、阴郁怪趣味。 Klei Don't Starve style: hand-ink outlines, slightly jittery line weight, flat or lightly hatched fills, desaturated earthy palette, puppet-like stylized proportions, subtle grim whimsy. NOT photoreal, NOT glossy anime cel, NOT soft airbrush beauty, NOT clean Pixar 3D. 主体设色：角色与装备用色鲜艳醒目、饱和度高，明暗与色块对比强烈、轮廓与色块交界利落；与虚化低饱和背景形成清晰层次分离，缩略图一眼可读。勿把全身涂成灰褐糊成一团。 Subject coloring: vivid saturated hues on character and gear, strong value/chroma contrast, crisp shapes; clear figure/ground separation from soft desaturated bokeh. Must read as a colorful silhouette at thumbnail size.  外观与设定要点：（表驱动补全）憎恶：剪影夸张、肢体略木偶化；装备/武器轮廓贴合名称与《魔兽世界》路人想象，避免写实电影脸。 出没于「模板兵种」战场的敌方单位；未知系，近战，战职偏输出。 以近战姿态做出代表性攻击预备或挥击瞬间；不必写技能名。 World of Warcraft fantasy creature, readable silhouette at thumbnail size, inked rim light not soft bloom. Avoid: circular badge UI frame, watermark, readable text, photoreal skin, glossy anime highlights, Octane 3D, busy sharp readable full dungeon map as background, gore. 设定标签（勿在画面写文字）：近战，其他，输出
```

NOT photoreal, NOT glossy anime cel, NOT soft airbrush beauty, NOT clean Pixar 3D. 主体设色：角色与装备用色鲜艳醒目、饱和度高，明暗与色块对比强烈、轮廓与色块交界利落；与虚化低饱和背景形成清晰层次分离，缩略图一眼可读。勿把全身涂成灰褐糊成一团。 Subject coloring: vivid saturated hues on character and gear, strong value/chroma contrast, crisp shapes; clear figure/ground separation from soft desaturated bokeh. NOT photoreal, NOT glossy anime cel, NOT soft airbrush beauty, NOT clean Pixar 3D. 主体设色：角色与装备用色鲜艳醒目、饱和度高，明暗与色块对比强烈、轮廓与色块交界利落；与虚化低饱和背景形成清晰层次分离，缩略图一眼可读。勿把全身涂成灰褐糊成一团。 Subject coloring: vivid saturated hues on character and gear, strong value/chroma contrast, crisp shapes; clear figure/ground separation from soft desaturated bokeh. Must read as a colorful silhouette at thumbnail size.  外观与设定要点：身着破烂红袍的人类信徒，脸上绘有燃烧的眼睛符文，手持匕首 燃刃教派的狂热信徒 暗影箭：发射暗影箭矢 World of Warcraft fantasy creature, readable silhouette at thumbnail size, inked rim light not soft bloom. Avoid: circular badge UI frame, watermark, readable text, photoreal skin, glossy anime highlights, Octane 3D, busy sharp readable full dungeon map as background, gore. 设定标签（勿在画面写文字）：远程，其他，增益

### 最终首领 — 提示词

- **首领**：奥格尔弗林特（Oggleflint）
- **类型**：关卡首领
- **bossUid**：`B000001`
- **表 id**：`boss_ch1_oggleflint`

```text
【关卡首领】奥格尔弗林特（Oggleflint）。地下城：怒焰裂谷 / Ragefire Chasm。关卡语境：怒焰裂谷-第一关。首领需要更强剪影与略大魄力，仍为饥荒手绘线稿风而非写实 Boss 海报。 背景为高度虚化的统一暗红与酒红 bokeh（#450a0a、#7f1d1d 系），阴郁低饱和、边缘略发黑，避免亮橙火焰铺满。 Heavily blurred bokeh background dominated by unified dark crimson and burgundy (#450a0a, #7f1d1d), ominous low saturation, slightly blackened edges, no bright orange flames. 【首领立绘硬性要求】背景必须是暗红/酒红虚化 bokeh，禁止冷灰、石板灰、蓝灰 bokeh；勿与小怪共用灰色背景。 MANDATORY for dungeon boss portrait: background MUST be dark crimson/burgundy bokeh only; NOT cool gray, slate, or blue-gray bokeh; NOT the same neutral gray as trash mobs. 饥荒（Don't Starve）/ Klei 手绘感：墨线勾边、线宽略抖、低饱和大地色系、平涂或轻排线、木偶感比例、阴郁怪趣味。 Klei Don't Starve style: hand-ink outlines, slightly jittery line weight, flat or lightly hatched fills, desaturated earthy palette, puppet-like stylized proportions, subtle grim whimsy. NOT photoreal, NOT glossy anime cel, NOT soft airbrush beauty, NOT clean Pixar 3D. 主体设色：角色与装备用色鲜艳醒目、饱和度高，明暗与色块对比强烈、轮廓与色块交界利落；与虚化低饱和背景形成清晰层次分离，缩略图一眼可读。勿把全身涂成灰褐糊成一团。 Subject coloring: vivid saturated hues on character and gear, strong value/chroma contrast, crisp shapes; clear figure/ground separation from soft desaturated bokeh. Must read as a colorful silhouette at thumbnail size.  设定要点：身材矮壮的穴居人，皮肤呈暗红焦岩色，双手粗糙有力 石质打击：物理伤害；冲锋：快速接近敌人 World of Warcraft dungeon boss portrait, dramatic puppet-like stylization, dark red burgundy bokeh background required. Avoid: circular badge UI frame, watermark, readable text, photoreal skin, glossy anime highlights, Octane 3D, busy sharp readable full dungeon map as background, gore. 设定标签（勿在画面写文字）：近战，其他，输出
```

```text
【书怪小怪｜死亡矿井（Deadmines）】迪菲亚船员（Defias Pirate）。魔兽世界地下城设定下的单体角色立绘或小场景胸像，方图构图、主体居中、剪影在缩略图尺度可读。 背景为高度虚化的统一冷灰 bokeh（石板灰 #94a3a8 系），低饱和、边缘略压暗炭灰 #475569，无职业色光晕、无整块抢镜彩色氛围。 Heavily blurred bokeh background dominated by unified cool neutral gray (#94a3a8, slate), low saturation, slightly darker charcoal #475569 at edges, no colored class glow. 饥荒（Don't Starve）/ Klei 手绘感：墨线勾边、线宽略抖、低饱和大地色系、平涂或轻排线、木偶感比例、阴郁怪趣味。 Klei Don't Starve style: hand-ink outlines, slightly jittery line weight, flat or lightly hatched fills, desaturated earthy palette, puppet-like stylized proportions, subtle grim whimsy. NOT photoreal, NOT glossy anime cel, NOT soft airbrush beauty, NOT clean Pixar 3D. 主体设色：角色与装备用色鲜艳醒目、饱和度高，明暗与色块对比强烈、轮廓与色块交界利落；与虚化低饱和背景形成清晰层次分离，缩略图一眼可读。勿把全身涂成灰褐糊成一团。 Subject coloring: vivid saturated hues on character and gear, strong value/chroma contrast, crisp shapes; clear figure/ground separation from soft desaturated bokeh. Must read as a colorful silhouette at thumbnail size.  外观与设定要点：身穿破旧海军服的人类海盗，头戴黑色三角帽，腰间别着弯刀 迪菲亚兄弟会的水手，精通近战搏斗 弯刀斩：挥舞弯刀劈砍 World of Warcraft fantasy creature, readable silhouette at thumbnail size, inked rim light not soft bloom. Avoid: circular badge UI frame, watermark, readable text, photoreal skin, glossy anime highlights, Octane 3D, busy sharp readable full dungeon map as background, gore. 设定标签（勿在画面写文字）：近战，生物，输出
```

### 最终首领 — 提示词

- **首领**：拉克佐（Rhahk'zor）
- **类型**：关卡首领
- **bossUid**：`B000005`
- **表 id**：`boss_ch5_rhahk_zor`

```text
【关卡首领】拉克佐（Rhahk'zor）。地下城：死亡矿井 / Deadmines。关卡语境：死亡矿井-第一关。首领需要更强剪影与略大魄力，仍为饥荒手绘线稿风而非写实 Boss 海报。 背景为高度虚化的统一暗红与酒红 bokeh（#450a0a、#7f1d1d 系），阴郁低饱和、边缘略发黑，避免亮橙火焰铺满。 Heavily blurred bokeh background dominated by unified dark crimson and burgundy (#450a0a, #7f1d1d), ominous low saturation, slightly blackened edges, no bright orange flames. 【首领立绘硬性要求】背景必须是暗红/酒红虚化 bokeh，禁止冷灰、石板灰、蓝灰 bokeh；勿与小怪共用灰色背景。 MANDATORY for dungeon boss portrait: background MUST be dark crimson/burgundy bokeh only; NOT cool gray, slate, or blue-gray bokeh; NOT the same neutral gray as trash mobs. 饥荒（Don't Starve）/ Klei 手绘感：墨线勾边、线宽略抖、低饱和大地色系、平涂或轻排线、木偶感比例、阴郁怪趣味。 Klei Don't Starve style: hand-ink outlines, slightly jittery line weight, flat or lightly hatched fills, desaturated earthy palette, puppet-like stylized proportions, subtle grim whimsy. NOT photoreal, NOT glossy anime cel, NOT soft airbrush beauty, NOT clean Pixar 3D. 主体设色：角色与装备用色鲜艳醒目、饱和度高，明暗与色块对比强烈、轮廓与色块交界利落；与虚化低饱和背景形成清晰层次分离，缩略图一眼可读。勿把全身涂成灰褐糊成一团。 Subject coloring: vivid saturated hues on character and gear, strong value/chroma contrast, crisp shapes; clear figure/ground separation from soft desaturated bokeh. Must read as a colorful silhouette at thumbnail size.  设定要点：身材魁梧的食人魔战士，肌肉虬结，手持巨大的战斧 猛击：造成大量物理伤害；顺劈斩：攻击面前多个敌人；战吼：提升自身攻击力 World of Warcraft dungeon boss portrait, dramatic puppet-like stylization, dark red burgundy bokeh background required. Avoid: circular badge UI frame, watermark, readable text, photoreal skin, glossy anime highlights, Octane 3D, busy sharp readable full dungeon map as background, gore. 设定标签（勿在画面写文字）：近战，生物，坦克
```

### 最终首领 — 提示词

- **首领**：毒蛇女士（Lady Anacondra）
- **类型**：关卡首领
- **bossUid**：`B000011`
- **表 id**：`boss_ch11_lady_anacondra`

```text
【关卡首领】毒蛇女士（Lady Anacondra）。地下城：哀嚎洞穴 / Wailing Caverns。关卡语境：哀嚎洞穴-第一关。首领需要更强剪影与略大魄力，仍为饥荒手绘线稿风而非写实 Boss 海报。 背景为高度虚化的统一暗红与酒红 bokeh（#450a0a、#7f1d1d 系），阴郁低饱和、边缘略发黑，避免亮橙火焰铺满。 Heavily blurred bokeh background dominated by unified dark crimson and burgundy (#450a0a, #7f1d1d), ominous low saturation, slightly blackened edges, no bright orange flames. 【首领立绘硬性要求】背景必须是暗红/酒红虚化 bokeh，禁止冷灰、石板灰、蓝灰 bokeh；勿与小怪共用灰色背景。 MANDATORY for dungeon boss portrait: background MUST be dark crimson/burgundy bokeh only; NOT cool gray, slate, or blue-gray bokeh; NOT the same neutral gray as trash mobs. 饥荒（Don't Starve）/ Klei 手绘感：墨线勾边、线宽略抖、低饱和大地色系、平涂或轻排线、木偶感比例、阴郁怪趣味。 Klei Don't Starve style: hand-ink outlines, slightly jittery line weight, flat or lightly hatched fills, desaturated earthy palette, puppet-like stylized proportions, subtle grim whimsy. NOT photoreal, NOT glossy anime cel, NOT soft airbrush beauty, NOT clean Pixar 3D. 主体设色：角色与装备用色鲜艳醒目、饱和度高，明暗与色块对比强烈、轮廓与色块交界利落；与虚化低饱和背景形成清晰层次分离，缩略图一眼可读。勿把全身涂成灰褐糊成一团。 Subject coloring: vivid saturated hues on character and gear, strong value/chroma contrast, crisp shapes; clear figure/ground separation from soft desaturated bokeh. Must read as a colorful silhouette at thumbnail size.  设定要点：身穿华丽长袍的女性蛇人德鲁伊，佩戴羽毛和骨头装饰，手持弯曲的法杖 闪电箭：发射闪电攻击；睡眠：使目标入睡；治疗之触：恢复友方生命值 World of Warcraft dungeon boss portrait, dramatic puppet-like stylization, dark red burgundy bokeh background required. Avoid: circular badge UI frame, watermark, readable text, photoreal skin, glossy anime highlights, Octane 3D, busy sharp readable full dungeon map as background, gore. 设定标签（勿在画面写文字）：远程，生物，辅助
```

```text
【关卡首领】眼镜蛇领主（Lord Serpentis）。地下城：哀嚎洞穴 / Wailing Caverns。关卡语境：哀嚎洞穴-第四关。首领需要更强剪影与略大魄力，仍为饥荒手绘线稿风而非写实 Boss 海报。 背景为高度虚化的统一暗红与酒红 bokeh（#450a0a、#7f1d1d 系），阴郁低饱和、边缘略发黑，避免亮橙火焰铺满。 Heavily blurred bokeh background dominated by unified dark crimson and burgundy (#450a0a, #7f1d1d), ominous low saturation, slightly blackened edges, no bright orange flames. 【首领立绘硬性要求】背景必须是暗红/酒红虚化 bokeh，禁止冷灰、石板灰、蓝灰 bokeh；勿与小怪共用灰色背景。 MANDATORY for dungeon boss portrait: background MUST be dark crimson/burgundy bokeh only; NOT cool gray, slate, or blue-gray bokeh; NOT the same neutral gray as trash mobs. 饥荒（Don't Starve）/ Klei 手绘感：墨线勾边、线宽略抖、低饱和大地色系、平涂或轻排线、木偶感比例、阴郁怪趣味。 Klei Don't Starve style: hand-ink outlines, slightly jittery line weight, flat or lightly hatched fills, desaturated earthy palette, puppet-like stylized proportions, subtle grim whimsy. NOT photoreal, NOT glossy anime cel, NOT soft airbrush beauty, NOT clean Pixar 3D. 主体设色：角色与装备用色鲜艳醒目、饱和度高，明暗与色块对比强烈、轮廓与色块交界利落；与虚化低饱和背景形成清晰层次分离，缩略图一眼可读。勿把全身涂成灰褐糊成一团。 Subject coloring: vivid saturated hues on character and gear, strong value/chroma contrast, crisp shapes; clear figure/ground separation from soft desaturated bokeh. Must read as a colorful silhouette at thumbnail size.  设定要点：身穿暗影长袍的蛇人法师，眼眸泛着幽光，手持魔杖 暗影箭：发射暗影箭矢；奥术飞弹：发射多枚魔法飞弹；法术反制：打断敌人施法 World of Warcraft dungeon boss portrait, dramatic puppet-like stylization, dark red burgundy bokeh background required. Avoid: circular badge UI frame, watermark, readable text, photoreal skin, glossy anime highlights, Octane 3D, busy sharp readable full dungeon map as background, gore. 设定标签（勿在画面写文字）：远程，生物，输出
```

```text

【书怪小怪｜影牙城堡（Shadowfang Keep）】暗影狼（Shadowfang Wolfguard）。魔兽世界地下城设定下的单体角色立绘或小场景胸像，方图构图、主体居中、剪影在缩略图尺度可读。 背景为高度虚化的统一冷灰 bokeh（石板灰 #94a3a8 系），低饱和、边缘略压暗炭灰 #475569，无职业色光晕、无整块抢镜彩色氛围。 Heavily blurred bokeh background dominated by unified cool neutral gray (#94a3a8, slate), low saturation, slightly darker charcoal #475569 at edges, no colored class glow. 饥荒（Don't Starve）/ Klei 手绘感：墨线勾边、线宽略抖、低饱和大地色系、平涂或轻排线、木偶感比例、阴郁怪趣味。 Klei Don't Starve style: hand-ink outlines, slightly jittery line weight, flat or lightly hatched fills, desaturated earthy palette, puppet-like stylized proportions, subtle grim whimsy. NOT photoreal, NOT glossy anime cel, NOT soft airbrush beauty, NOT clean Pixar 3D. 主体设色：角色与装备用色鲜艳醒目、饱和度高，明暗与色块对比强烈、轮廓与色块交界利落；与虚化低饱和背景形成清晰层次分离，缩略图一眼可读。勿把全身涂成灰褐糊成一团。 Subject coloring: vivid saturated hues on character and gear, strong value/chroma contrast, crisp shapes; clear figure/ground separation from soft desaturated bokeh. Must read as a colorful silhouette at thumbnail size.  外观与设定要点：暗影形态的狼，体型健壮 阿鲁高召唤的狼人守卫 爪击：用利爪撕裂 World of Warcraft fantasy creature, readable silhouette at thumbnail size, inked rim light not soft bloom. ```
```

### 最终首领 — 提示词

- **首领**：雷西戈尔（Rethilgore）
- **类型**：关卡首领
- **bossUid**：`B000017`
- **表 id**：`boss_ch17_rethilgore`

```text
【关卡首领】雷西戈尔（Rethilgore）。地下城：影牙城堡 / Shadowfang Keep。关卡语境：影牙城堡-第一关。首领需要更强剪影与略大魄力，仍为饥荒手绘线稿风而非写实 Boss 海报。 背景为高度虚化的统一暗红与酒红 bokeh（#450a0a、#7f1d1d 系），阴郁低饱和、边缘略发黑，避免亮橙火焰铺满。 Heavily blurred bokeh background dominated by unified dark crimson and burgundy (#450a0a, #7f1d1d), ominous low saturation, slightly blackened edges, no bright orange flames. 【首领立绘硬性要求】背景必须是暗红/酒红虚化 bokeh，禁止冷灰、石板灰、蓝灰 bokeh；勿与小怪共用灰色背景。 MANDATORY for dungeon boss portrait: background MUST be dark crimson/burgundy bokeh only; NOT cool gray, slate, or blue-gray bokeh; NOT the same neutral gray as trash mobs. 饥荒（Don't Starve）/ Klei 手绘感：墨线勾边、线宽略抖、低饱和大地色系、平涂或轻排线、木偶感比例、阴郁怪趣味。 Klei Don't Starve style: hand-ink outlines, slightly jittery line weight, flat or lightly hatched fills, desaturated earthy palette, puppet-like stylized proportions, subtle grim whimsy. NOT photoreal, NOT glossy anime cel, NOT soft airbrush beauty, NOT clean Pixar 3D. 主体设色：角色与装备用色鲜艳醒目、饱和度高，明暗与色块对比强烈、轮廓与色块交界利落；与虚化低饱和背景形成清晰层次分离，缩略图一眼可读。勿把全身涂成灰褐糊成一团。 Subject coloring: vivid saturated hues on character and gear, strong value/chroma contrast, crisp shapes; clear figure/ground separation from soft desaturated bokeh. Must read as a colorful silhouette at thumbnail size.  设定要点：狼人形态的猎手首领，灰褐色毛发，眼中泛着红光，手持巨斧 灵魂虹吸：偷取目标生命值；虚弱诅咒：降低敌人属性；嚎叫：发出恐惧嚎叫 World of Warcraft dungeon boss portrait, dramatic puppet-like stylization, dark red burgundy bokeh background required. Avoid: circular badge UI frame, watermark, readable text, photoreal skin, glossy anime highlights, Octane 3D, busy sharp readable full dungeon map as background, gore. 设定标签（勿在画面写文字）：近战，生物，输出
```

- **表 id**：`boss_ch23_archmage_arugal`

```text
【最终首领】大法师阿鲁高（Archmage Arugal）。地下城：影牙城堡 / Shadowfang Keep。关卡语境：影牙城堡-第七关。首领需要更强剪影与略大魄力，仍为饥荒手绘线稿风而非写实 Boss 海报。 背景为高度虚化的统一暗红与酒红 bokeh（#450a0a、#7f1d1d 系），阴郁低饱和、边缘略发黑，避免亮橙火焰铺满。 Heavily blurred bokeh background dominated by unified dark crimson and burgundy (#450a0a, #7f1d1d), ominous low saturation, slightly blackened edges, no bright orange flames. 【首领立绘硬性要求】背景必须是暗红/酒红虚化 bokeh，禁止冷灰、石板灰、蓝灰 bokeh；勿与小怪共用灰色背景。 MANDATORY for dungeon boss portrait: background MUST be dark crimson/burgundy bokeh only; NOT cool gray, slate, or blue-gray bokeh; NOT the same neutral gray as trash mobs. 饥荒（Don't Starve）/ Klei 手绘感：墨线勾边、线宽略抖、低饱和大地色系、平涂或轻排线、木偶感比例、阴郁怪趣味。 Klei Don't Starve style: hand-ink outlines, slightly jittery line weight, flat or lightly hatched fills, desaturated earthy palette, puppet-like stylized proportions, subtle grim whimsy. NOT photoreal, NOT glossy anime cel, NOT soft airbrush beauty, NOT clean Pixar 3D. 主体设色：角色与装备用色鲜艳醒目、饱和度高，明暗与色块对比强烈、轮廓与色块交界利落；与虚化低饱和背景形成清晰层次分离，缩略图一眼可读。勿把全身涂成灰褐糊成一团。 Subject coloring: vivid saturated hues on character and gear, strong value/chroma contrast, crisp shapes; clear figure/ground separation from soft desaturated bokeh. Must read as a colorful silhouette at thumbnail size.  设定要点：身穿紫色长袍的人类法师，眼窝深陷，周围环绕着扭曲的魔法能量 奥术飞弹：发射多枚奥术能量球；变形术：变成小动物；召唤狼人：召唤狼人仆从；奥术爆炸：范围伤害 World of Warcraft dungeon boss portrait, dramatic puppet-like stylization, dark red burgundy bokeh background required. Avoid: circular badge UI frame, watermark, readable text, photoreal skin, glossy anime highlights, Octane 3D, busy sharp readable full dungeon map as background, gore. 设定标签（勿在画面写文字）：远程，生物，输出
```

NOT photoreal, NOT glossy anime cel, NOT soft airbrush beauty, NOT clean Pixar 3D. 主体设色：角色与装备用色鲜艳醒目、饱和度高，明暗与色块对比强烈、轮廓与色块交界利落；与虚化低饱和背景形成清晰层次分离，缩略图一眼可读。勿把全身涂成灰褐糊成一团。 Subject coloring: vivid saturated hues on character and gear, strong value/chroma contrast, crisp shapes; clear figure/ground separation from soft desaturated bokeh. Must read as a colorful silhouette at thumbnail size.  外观与设定要点：人身蛇尾的娜迦侍从 娜迦的普通成员 水溅：用尾巴拍击 World of Warcraft fantasy creature, readable silhouette at thumbnail size, inked rim light not soft bloom. Avoid: circular badge UI frame, watermark, readable text, photoreal skin, glossy anime highlights, Octane 3D, busy sharp readable full dungeon map as background, gore. 设定标签（勿在画面写文字）：近战，生物，输出

### 最终首领 — 提示词

- **首领**：加穆-拉（Ghamoo-Ra）
- **类型**：关卡首领
- **bossUid**：`B000024`
- **表 id**：`boss_ch24_ghamoo_ra`

```text
【关卡首领】加穆-拉（Ghamoo-Ra）。地下城：黑暗深渊 / Blackfathom Deeps。关卡语境：黑暗深渊-第一关。首领需要更强剪影与略大魄力，仍为饥荒手绘线稿风而非写实 Boss 海报。 背景为高度虚化的统一暗红与酒红 bokeh（#450a0a、#7f1d1d 系），阴郁低饱和、边缘略发黑，避免亮橙火焰铺满。 Heavily blurred bokeh background dominated by unified dark crimson and burgundy (#450a0a, #7f1d1d), ominous low saturation, slightly blackened edges, no bright orange flames. 【首领立绘硬性要求】背景必须是暗红/酒红虚化 bokeh，禁止冷灰、石板灰、蓝灰 bokeh；勿与小怪共用灰色背景。 MANDATORY for dungeon boss portrait: background MUST be dark crimson/burgundy bokeh only; NOT cool gray, slate, or blue-gray bokeh; NOT the same neutral gray as trash mobs. 饥荒（Don't Starve）/ Klei 手绘感：墨线勾边、线宽略抖、低饱和大地色系、平涂或轻排线、木偶感比例、阴郁怪趣味。 Klei Don't Starve style: hand-ink outlines, slightly jittery line weight, flat or lightly hatched fills, desaturated earthy palette, puppet-like stylized proportions, subtle grim whimsy. NOT photoreal, NOT glossy anime cel, NOT soft airbrush beauty, NOT clean Pixar 3D. 主体设色：角色与装备用色鲜艳醒目、饱和度高，明暗与色块对比强烈、轮廓与色块交界利落；与虚化低饱和背景形成清晰层次分离，缩略图一眼可读。勿把全身涂成灰褐糊成一团。 Subject coloring: vivid saturated hues on character and gear, strong value/chroma contrast, crisp shapes; clear figure/ground separation from soft desaturated bokeh. Must read as a colorful silhouette at thumbnail size.  设定要点：巨大的海龟形态生物，龟壳由深蓝色岩石构成，体型巨大如小山 碾压：用巨大身躯压向敌人；水溅：用尾巴拍击造成范围伤害；龟甲防御：减免伤害 World of Warcraft dungeon boss portrait, dramatic puppet-like stylization, dark red burgundy bokeh background required. Avoid: circular badge UI frame, watermark, readable text, photoreal skin, glossy anime highlights, Octane 3D, busy sharp readable full dungeon map as background, gore. 设定标签（勿在画面写文字）：近战，其他，坦克
```

- **表 id**：`boss_ch31_aku_mai_the_devourer`

```text
【最终首领】吞噬者阿库迈尔（Aku'mai the Devourer）。地下城：黑暗深渊 / Blackfathom Deeps。关卡语境：黑暗深渊-第八关。首领需要更强剪影与略大魄力，仍为饥荒手绘线稿风而非写实 Boss 海报。 背景为高度虚化的统一暗红与酒红 bokeh（#450a0a、#7f1d1d 系），阴郁低饱和、边缘略发黑，避免亮橙火焰铺满。 Heavily blurred bokeh background dominated by unified dark crimson and burgundy (#450a0a, #7f1d1d), ominous low saturation, slightly blackened edges, no bright orange flames. 【首领立绘硬性要求】背景必须是暗红/酒红虚化 bokeh，禁止冷灰、石板灰、蓝灰 bokeh；勿与小怪共用灰色背景。 MANDATORY for dungeon boss portrait: background MUST be dark crimson/burgundy bokeh only; NOT cool gray, slate, or blue-gray bokeh; NOT the same neutral gray as trash mobs. 饥荒（Don't Starve）/ Klei 手绘感：墨线勾边、线宽略抖、低饱和大地色系、平涂或轻排线、木偶感比例、阴郁怪趣味。 Klei Don't Starve style: hand-ink outlines, slightly jittery line weight, flat or lightly hatched fills, desaturated earthy palette, puppet-like stylized proportions, subtle grim whimsy. NOT photoreal, NOT glossy anime cel, NOT soft airbrush beauty, NOT clean Pixar 3D. 主体设色：角色与装备用色鲜艳醒目、饱和度高，明暗与色块对比强烈、轮廓与色块交界利落；与虚化低饱和背景形成清晰层次分离，缩略图一眼可读。勿把全身涂成灰褐糊成一团。 Subject coloring: vivid saturated hues on character and gear, strong value/chroma contrast, crisp shapes; clear figure/ground separation from soft desaturated bokeh. Must read as a colorful silhouette at thumbnail size.  设定要点：巨大的克拉西斯生物，体型庞大，全身覆盖深蓝色的甲壳，触手众多 吞噬：造成伤害并恢复生命值；深渊吐息：喷出黑暗能量；尾击：横扫身后敌人；黑暗护盾：吸收伤害 World of Warcraft dungeon boss portrait, dramatic puppet-like stylization, dark red burgundy bokeh background required. Avoid: circular badge UI frame, watermark, readable text, photoreal skin, glossy anime highlights, Octane 3D, busy sharp readable full dungeon map as background, gore. 设定标签（勿在画面写文字）：近战，其他，坦克
```

```text
【书怪小怪｜诺莫瑞根（Gnomeregan）】麻风侏儒（Leper Gnome）。魔兽世界地下城设定下的单体角色立绘或小场景胸像，方图构图、主体居中、剪影在缩略图尺度可读。 背景为高度虚化的统一冷灰 bokeh（石板灰 #94a3a8 系），低饱和、边缘略压暗炭灰 #475569，无职业色光晕、无整块抢镜彩色氛围。 Heavily blurred bokeh background dominated by unified cool neutral gray (#94a3a8, slate), low saturation, slightly darker charcoal #475569 at edges, no colored class glow. 饥荒（Don't Starve）/ Klei 手绘感：墨线勾边、线宽略抖、低饱和大地色系、平涂或轻排线、木偶感比例、阴郁怪趣味。 Klei Don't Starve style: hand-ink outlines, slightly jittery line weight, flat or lightly hatched fills, desaturated earthy palette, puppet-like stylized proportions, subtle grim whimsy. NOT photoreal, NOT glossy anime cel, NOT soft airbrush beauty, NOT clean Pixar 3D. 主体设色：角色与装备用色鲜艳醒目、饱和度高，明暗与色块对比强烈、轮廓与色块交界利落；与虚化低饱和背景形成清晰层次分离，缩略图一眼可读。勿把全身涂成灰褐糊成一团。 Subject coloring: vivid saturated hues on character and gear, strong value/chroma contrast, crisp shapes; clear figure/ground separation from soft desaturated bokeh. Must read as a colorful silhouette at thumbnail size.  外观与设定要点：身患麻风的侏儒，身体溃烂但仍能战斗 被疾病折磨的侏儒 腐化攻击：造成持续自然伤害 World of Warcraft fantasy creature, readable silhouette at thumbnail size, inked rim light not soft bloom. Avoid: circular badge UI frame, watermark, readable text, photoreal skin, glossy anime highlights, Octane 3D, busy sharp readable full dungeon map as background, gore. 设定标签（勿在画面写文字）：近战，其他，输出
```

### 最终首领 — 提示词

- **bossUid**：`B000032`
- **表 id**：`boss_ch32_grubbis`

```text
【关卡首领】格鲁比斯（Grubbis）。地下城：诺莫瑞根 / Gnomeregan。关卡语境：诺莫瑞根-第一关。首领需要更强剪影与略大魄力，仍为饥荒手绘线稿风而非写实 Boss 海报。 背景为高度虚化的统一暗红与酒红 bokeh（#450a0a、#7f1d1d 系），阴郁低饱和、边缘略发黑，避免亮橙火焰铺满。 Heavily blurred bokeh background dominated by unified dark crimson and burgundy (#450a0a, #7f1d1d), ominous low saturation, slightly blackened edges, no bright orange flames. 【首领立绘硬性要求】背景必须是暗红/酒红虚化 bokeh，禁止冷灰、石板灰、蓝灰 bokeh；勿与小怪共用灰色背景。 MANDATORY for dungeon boss portrait: background MUST be dark crimson/burgundy bokeh only; NOT cool gray, slate, or blue-gray bokeh; NOT the same neutral gray as trash mobs. 饥荒（Don't Starve）/ Klei 手绘感：墨线勾边、线宽略抖、低饱和大地色系、平涂或轻排线、木偶感比例、阴郁怪趣味。 Klei Don't Starve style: hand-ink outlines, slightly jittery line weight, flat or lightly hatched fills, desaturated earthy palette, puppet-like stylized proportions, subtle grim whimsy. NOT photoreal, NOT glossy anime cel, NOT soft airbrush beauty, NOT clean Pixar 3D. 主体设色：角色与装备用色鲜艳醒目、饱和度高，明暗与色块对比强烈、轮廓与色块交界利落；与虚化低饱和背景形成清晰层次分离，缩略图一眼可读。勿把全身涂成灰褐糊成一团。 Subject coloring: vivid saturated hues on character and gear, strong value/chroma contrast, crisp shapes; clear figure/ground separation from soft desaturated bokeh. Must read as a colorful silhouette at thumbnail size.  设定要点：变异的穴居人，体型是普通穴居人的两倍，皮肤呈病态绿色，全身覆盖甲壳 辐射吐息：喷出辐射性液体；酸液喷射：酸性吐息腐蚀护甲；狂暴冲撞：冲向敌人造成伤害 World of Warcraft dungeon boss portrait, dramatic puppet-like stylization, dark red burgundy bokeh background required. ### 最终首领 — 提示词
```

- **首领**：鲁古格（Roogug）
- **类型**：关卡首领
- **bossUid**：`B000037`
- **表 id**：`boss_ch37_roogug`

```text
【关卡首领】鲁古格（Roogug）。地下城：剃刀沼泽 / Razorfen Kraul。关卡语境：剃刀沼泽-第一关。首领需要更强剪影与略大魄力，仍为饥荒手绘线稿风而非写实 Boss 海报。 背景为高度虚化的统一暗红与酒红 bokeh（#450a0a、#7f1d1d 系），阴郁低饱和、边缘略发黑，避免亮橙火焰铺满。 Heavily blurred bokeh background dominated by unified dark crimson and burgundy (#450a0a, #7f1d1d), ominous low saturation, slightly blackened edges, no bright orange flames. 【首领立绘硬性要求】背景必须是暗红/酒红虚化 bokeh，禁止冷灰、石板灰、蓝灰 bokeh；勿与小怪共用灰色背景。 MANDATORY for dungeon boss portrait: background MUST be dark crimson/burgundy bokeh only; NOT cool gray, slate, or blue-gray bokeh; NOT the same neutral gray as trash mobs. 饥荒（Don't Starve）/ Klei 手绘感：墨线勾边、线宽略抖、低饱和大地色系、平涂或轻排线、木偶感比例、阴郁怪趣味。 Klei Don't Starve style: hand-ink outlines, slightly jittery line weight, flat or lightly hatched fills, desaturated earthy palette, puppet-like stylized proportions, subtle grim whimsy. NOT photoreal, NOT glossy anime cel, NOT soft airbrush beauty, NOT clean Pixar 3D. 主体设色：角色与装备用色鲜艳醒目、饱和度高，明暗与色块对比强烈、轮廓与色块交界利落；与虚化低饱和背景形成清晰层次分离，缩略图一眼可读。勿把全身涂成灰褐糊成一团。 Subject coloring: vivid saturated hues on character and gear, strong value/chroma contrast, crisp shapes; clear figure/ground separation from soft desaturated bokeh. Must read as a colorful silhouette at thumbnail size.  设定要点：野猪人萨满，佩戴骨头装饰，手持法杖，能召唤元素 闪电箭：发射闪电攻击；治疗波：恢复友方生命值；土元素召唤：召唤土元素协助 World of Warcraft dungeon boss portrait, dramatic puppet-like stylization, dark red burgundy bokeh background required. Avoid: circular badge UI frame, watermark, readable text, photoreal skin, glossy anime highlights, Octane 3D, busy sharp readable full dungeon map as background, gore. 设定标签（勿在画面写文字）：远程，生物，辅助
```

- **表 id**：`boss_ch38_aggem_thorncurse`

```text
【关卡首领】阿格姆·索恩克尔斯（Aggem Thorncurse）。地下城：剃刀沼泽 / Razorfen Kraul。关卡语境：剃刀沼泽-第二关。首领需要更强剪影与略大魄力，仍为饥荒手绘线稿风而非写实 Boss 海报。 背景为高度虚化的统一暗红与酒红 bokeh（#450a0a、#7f1d1d 系），阴郁低饱和、边缘略发黑，避免亮橙火焰铺满。 Heavily blurred bokeh background dominated by unified dark crimson and burgundy (#450a0a, #7f1d1d), ominous low saturation, slightly blackened edges, no bright orange flames. 【首领立绘硬性要求】背景必须是暗红/酒红虚化 bokeh，禁止冷灰、石板灰、蓝灰 bokeh；勿与小怪共用灰色背景。 MANDATORY for dungeon boss portrait: background MUST be dark crimson/burgundy bokeh only; NOT cool gray, slate, or blue-gray bokeh; NOT the same neutral gray as trash mobs. 饥荒（Don't Starve）/ Klei 手绘感：墨线勾边、线宽略抖、低饱和大地色系、平涂或轻排线、木偶感比例、阴郁怪趣味。 Klei Don't Starve style: hand-ink outlines, slightly jittery line weight, flat or lightly hatched fills, desaturated earthy palette, puppet-like stylized proportions, subtle grim whimsy. NOT photoreal, NOT glossy anime cel, NOT soft airbrush beauty, NOT clean Pixar 3D. 主体设色：角色与装备用色鲜艳醒目、饱和度高，明暗与色块对比强烈、轮廓与色块交界利落；与虚化低饱和背景形成清晰层次分离，缩略图一眼可读。勿把全身涂成灰褐糊成一团。 Subject coloring: vivid saturated hues on character and gear, strong value/chroma contrast, crisp shapes; clear figure/ground separation from soft desaturated bokeh. Must read as a colorful silhouette at thumbnail size.  设定要点：野猪人野兽大师，身边跟随着多只野猪，手持长矛和匕首 召唤野猪：召唤野猪仆从；协同攻击：指挥野猪同时攻击；战栗：恐惧周围敌人 World of Warcraft dungeon boss portrait, dramatic puppet-like stylization, dark red burgundy bokeh background required. Avoid: circular badge UI frame, watermark, readable text, photoreal skin, glossy anime highlights, Octane 3D, busy sharp readable full dungeon map as background, gore. 设定标签（勿在画面写文字）：近战，生物，输出
```

NOT photoreal, NOT glossy anime cel, NOT soft airbrush beauty, NOT clean Pixar 3D. 主体设色：角色与装备用色鲜艳醒目、饱和度高，明暗与色块对比强烈、轮廓与色块交界利落；与虚化低饱和背景形成清晰层次分离，缩略图一眼可读。勿把全身涂成灰褐糊成一团。 Subject coloring: vivid saturated hues on character and gear, strong value/chroma contrast, crisp shapes; clear figure/ground separation from soft desaturated bokeh. Must read as a colorful silhouette at thumbnail size.  外观与设定要点：身披红色祭袍的牧师，手持圣典 血色十字军的精神领袖 治疗：恢复友方生命值 World of Warcraft fantasy creature, readable silhouette at thumbnail size, inked rim light not soft bloom. Avoid: circular badge UI frame, watermark, readable text, photoreal skin, glossy anime highlights, Octane 3D, busy sharp readable full dungeon map as background, gore. 设定标签（勿在画面写文字）：远程，生物，辅助

### 最终首领 — 提示词

- **首领**：灵魂收割者萨尔诺斯（Thalnos the Soulrender）
- **类型**：关卡首领
- **bossUid**：`B000043`
- **表 id**：`boss_ch43_thalnos_the_soulrender`

```text
【关卡首领】灵魂收割者萨尔诺斯（Thalnos the Soulrender）。地下城：血色修道院 / Scarlet Monastery。关卡语境：血色修道院-第一关。首领需要更强剪影与略大魄力，仍为饥荒手绘线稿风而非写实 Boss 海报。 背景为高度虚化的统一暗红与酒红 bokeh（#450a0a、#7f1d1d 系），阴郁低饱和、边缘略发黑，避免亮橙火焰铺满。 Heavily blurred bokeh background dominated by unified dark crimson and burgundy (#450a0a, #7f1d1d), ominous low saturation, slightly blackened edges, no bright orange flames. 【首领立绘硬性要求】背景必须是暗红/酒红虚化 bokeh，禁止冷灰、石板灰、蓝灰 bokeh；勿与小怪共用灰色背景。 MANDATORY for dungeon boss portrait: background MUST be dark crimson/burgundy bokeh only; NOT cool gray, slate, or blue-gray bokeh; NOT the same neutral gray as trash mobs. 饥荒（Don't Starve）/ Klei 手绘感：墨线勾边、线宽略抖、低饱和大地色系、平涂或轻排线、木偶感比例、阴郁怪趣味。 Klei Don't Starve style: hand-ink outlines, slightly jittery line weight, flat or lightly hatched fills, desaturated earthy palette, puppet-like stylized proportions, subtle grim whimsy. NOT photoreal, NOT glossy anime cel, NOT soft airbrush beauty, NOT clean Pixar 3D. 主体设色：角色与装备用色鲜艳醒目、饱和度高，明暗与色块对比强烈、轮廓与色块交界利落；与虚化低饱和背景形成清晰层次分离，缩略图一眼可读。勿把全身涂成灰褐糊成一团。 Subject coloring: vivid saturated hues on character and gear, strong value/chroma contrast, crisp shapes; clear figure/ground separation from soft desaturated bokeh. Must read as a colorful silhouette at thumbnail size.  设定要点：身穿破烂红袍的亡灵法师，眼窝中燃烧着蓝火，手持骷髅法杖 暗影箭：发射暗影箭矢；灵魂虹吸：偷取目标生命值；召唤骷髅：召唤亡灵仆从 World of Warcraft dungeon boss portrait, dramatic puppet-like stylization, dark red burgundy bokeh background required. Avoid: circular badge UI frame, watermark, readable text, photoreal skin, glossy anime highlights, Octane 3D, busy sharp readable full dungeon map as background, gore. 设定标签（勿在画面写文字）：远程，亡灵，输出
```

### 最终首领 — 提示词

- **首领**：奥鲁克斯（Aarux）
- **类型**：关卡首领
- **bossUid**：`B000046`
- **表 id**：`boss_ch46_aarux`

```text
【关卡首领】奥鲁克斯（Aarux）。地下城：剃刀高地 / Razorfen Downs。关卡语境：剃刀高地-第一关。首领需要更强剪影与略大魄力，仍为饥荒手绘线稿风而非写实 Boss 海报。 背景为高度虚化的统一暗红与酒红 bokeh（#450a0a、#7f1d1d 系），阴郁低饱和、边缘略发黑，避免亮橙火焰铺满。 Heavily blurred bokeh background dominated by unified dark crimson and burgundy (#450a0a, #7f1d1d), ominous low saturation, slightly blackened edges, no bright orange flames. 【首领立绘硬性要求】背景必须是暗红/酒红虚化 bokeh，禁止冷灰、石板灰、蓝灰 bokeh；勿与小怪共用灰色背景。 MANDATORY for dungeon boss portrait: background MUST be dark crimson/burgundy bokeh only; NOT cool gray, slate, or blue-gray bokeh; NOT the same neutral gray as trash mobs. 饥荒（Don't Starve）/ Klei 手绘感：墨线勾边、线宽略抖、低饱和大地色系、平涂或轻排线、木偶感比例、阴郁怪趣味。 Klei Don't Starve style: hand-ink outlines, slightly jittery line weight, flat or lightly hatched fills, desaturated earthy palette, puppet-like stylized proportions, subtle grim whimsy. NOT photoreal, NOT glossy anime cel, NOT soft airbrush beauty, NOT clean Pixar 3D. 主体设色：角色与装备用色鲜艳醒目、饱和度高，明暗与色块对比强烈、轮廓与色块交界利落；与虚化低饱和背景形成清晰层次分离，缩略图一眼可读。勿把全身涂成灰褐糊成一团。 Subject coloring: vivid saturated hues on character and gear, strong value/chroma contrast, crisp shapes; clear figure/ground separation from soft desaturated bokeh. Must read as a colorful silhouette at thumbnail size.  设定要点：半透明的幽灵野猪人，散发着冰冷的气息，手持幽灵之剑 灵魂冲击：穿透敌人造成伤害；寒意侵蚀：降低敌人攻击速度；幽灵护甲：减免伤害 World of Warcraft dungeon boss portrait, dramatic puppet-like stylization, dark red burgundy bokeh background required. Avoid: circular badge UI frame, watermark, readable text, photoreal skin, glossy anime highlights, Octane 3D, busy sharp readable full dungeon map as background, gore. 设定标签（勿在画面写文字）：近战，亡灵，输出
```

- **bossUid**：`B000047`
- **表 id**：`boss_ch47_mordresh_fire_eye`

```text
【关卡首领】火焰之眼莫德雷什（Mordresh Fire Eye）。地下城：剃刀高地 / Razorfen Downs。关卡语境：剃刀高地-第二关。首领需要更强剪影与略大魄力，仍为饥荒手绘线稿风而非写实 Boss 海报。 背景为高度虚化的统一暗红与酒红 bokeh（#450a0a、#7f1d1d 系），阴郁低饱和、边缘略发黑，避免亮橙火焰铺满。 Heavily blurred bokeh background dominated by unified dark crimson and burgundy (#450a0a, #7f1d1d), ominous low saturation, slightly blackened edges, no bright orange flames. 【首领立绘硬性要求】背景必须是暗红/酒红虚化 bokeh，禁止冷灰、石板灰、蓝灰 bokeh；勿与小怪共用灰色背景。 MANDATORY for dungeon boss portrait: background MUST be dark crimson/burgundy bokeh only; NOT cool gray, slate, or blue-gray bokeh; NOT the same neutral gray as trash mobs. 饥荒（Don't Starve）/ Klei 手绘感：墨线勾边、线宽略抖、低饱和大地色系、平涂或轻排线、木偶感比例、阴郁怪趣味。 Klei Don't Starve style: hand-ink outlines, slightly jittery line weight, flat or lightly hatched fills, desaturated earthy palette, puppet-like stylized proportions, subtle grim whimsy. NOT photoreal, NOT glossy anime cel, NOT soft airbrush beauty, NOT clean Pixar 3D. 主体设色：角色与装备用色鲜艳醒目、饱和度高，明暗与色块对比强烈、轮廓与色块交界利落；与虚化低饱和背景形成清晰层次分离，缩略图一眼可读。勿把全身涂成灰褐糊成一团。 Subject coloring: vivid saturated hues on character and gear, strong value/chroma contrast, crisp shapes; clear figure/ground separation from soft desaturated bokeh. Must read as a colorful silhouette at thumbnail size.  设定要点：巨大的骷髅战士，眼窝中燃烧着火焰，手持燃烧的战斧 火焰冲击：冲撞并造成火焰伤害；燃烧光环：周围持续受到火焰伤害；火焰弹：发射火球 World of Warcraft dungeon boss portrait, dramatic puppet-like stylization, dark red burgundy bokeh background required. Avoid: circular badge UI frame, watermark, readable text, photoreal skin, glossy anime highlights, Octane 3D, busy sharp readable full dungeon map as background, gore. 设定标签（勿在画面写文字）：近战，亡灵，输出
```

Must read as a colorful silhouette at thumbnail size.  外观与设定要点：被遗忘在矿洞中的矿工骷髅，手持生锈的镐头 死于矿难的不幸矿工 镐击：用矿镐攻击 World of Warcraft fantasy creature, readable silhouette at thumbnail size, inked rim light not soft bloom. Avoid: circular badge UI frame, watermark, readable text, photoreal skin, glossy anime highlights, Octane 3D, busy sharp readable full dungeon map as background, gore. 设定标签（勿在画面写文字）：近战，亡灵，输出

### 最终首领 — 提示词

- **首领**：雷维洛什（Revelosh）
- **类型**：关卡首领
- **bossUid**：`B000051`
- **表 id**：`boss_ch51_revelosh`

```text
【关卡首领】雷维洛什（Revelosh）。地下城：奥达曼 / Uldaman。关卡语境：奥达曼-第一关。首领需要更强剪影与略大魄力，仍为饥荒手绘线稿风而非写实 Boss 海报。 背景为高度虚化的统一暗红与酒红 bokeh（#450a0a、#7f1d1d 系），阴郁低饱和、边缘略发黑，避免亮橙火焰铺满。 Heavily blurred bokeh background dominated by unified dark crimson and burgundy (#450a0a, #7f1d1d), ominous low saturation, slightly blackened edges, no bright orange flames. 【首领立绘硬性要求】背景必须是暗红/酒红虚化 bokeh，禁止冷灰、石板灰、蓝灰 bokeh；勿与小怪共用灰色背景。 MANDATORY for dungeon boss portrait: background MUST be dark crimson/burgundy bokeh only; NOT cool gray, slate, or blue-gray bokeh; NOT the same neutral gray as trash mobs. 饥荒（Don't Starve）/ Klei 手绘感：墨线勾边、线宽略抖、低饱和大地色系、平涂或轻排线、木偶感比例、阴郁怪趣味。 Klei Don't Starve style: hand-ink outlines, slightly jittery line weight, flat or lightly hatched fills, desaturated earthy palette, puppet-like stylized proportions, subtle grim whimsy. NOT photoreal, NOT glossy anime cel, NOT soft airbrush beauty, NOT clean Pixar 3D. 主体设色：角色与装备用色鲜艳醒目、饱和度高，明暗与色块对比强烈、轮廓与色块交界利落；与虚化低饱和背景形成清晰层次分离，缩略图一眼可读。勿把全身涂成灰褐糊成一团。 Subject coloring: vivid saturated hues on character and gear, strong value/chroma contrast, crisp shapes; clear figure/ground separation from soft desaturated bokeh. Must read as a colorful silhouette at thumbnail size.  设定要点：由岩石构成的机械人偶，全身由青铜和钢铁构成，关节处有齿轮 机械拳击：用金属拳头攻击；电流冲击：释放电能攻击；修复：自我修复 World of Warcraft dungeon boss portrait, dramatic puppet-like stylization, dark red burgundy bokeh background required. Avoid: circular badge UI frame, watermark, readable text, photoreal skin, glossy anime highlights, Octane 3D, busy sharp readable full dungeon map as background, gore. 设定标签（勿在画面写文字）：近战，其他，输出
```

```text
【关卡首领】加尔甘·火锤（Galgann Firehammer）。地下城：奥达曼 / Uldaman。关卡语境：奥达曼-第五关。首领需要更强剪影与略大魄力，仍为饥荒手绘线稿风而非写实 Boss 海报。 背景为高度虚化的统一暗红与酒红 bokeh（#450a0a、#7f1d1d 系），阴郁低饱和、边缘略发黑，避免亮橙火焰铺满。 Heavily blurred bokeh background dominated by unified dark crimson and burgundy (#450a0a, #7f1d1d), ominous low saturation, slightly blackened edges, no bright orange flames. 【首领立绘硬性要求】背景必须是暗红/酒红虚化 bokeh，禁止冷灰、石板灰、蓝灰 bokeh；勿与小怪共用灰色背景。 MANDATORY for dungeon boss portrait: background MUST be dark crimson/burgundy bokeh only; NOT cool gray, slate, or blue-gray bokeh; NOT the same neutral gray as trash mobs. 饥荒（Don't Starve）/ Klei 手绘感：墨线勾边、线宽略抖、低饱和大地色系、平涂或轻排线、木偶感比例、阴郁怪趣味。 Klei Don't Starve style: hand-ink outlines, slightly jittery line weight, flat or lightly hatched fills, desaturated earthy palette, puppet-like stylized proportions, subtle grim whimsy. NOT photoreal, NOT glossy anime cel, NOT soft airbrush beauty, NOT clean Pixar 3D. 主体设色：角色与装备用色鲜艳醒目、饱和度高，明暗与色块对比强烈、轮廓与色块交界利落；与虚化低饱和背景形成清晰层次分离，缩略图一眼可读。勿把全身涂成灰褐糊成一团。 Subject coloring: vivid saturated hues on character and gear, strong value/chroma contrast, crisp shapes; clear figure/ground separation from soft desaturated bokeh. Must read as a colorful silhouette at thumbnail size.  设定要点：火焰元素的化身，全身由熔岩和火焰构成，手持燃烧的战锤 熔岩拳：用熔岩拳头攻击；火焰爆发：从身体爆发火焰；炽热光环：周围持续受到火焰伤害 World of Warcraft dungeon boss portrait, dramatic puppet-like stylization, dark red burgundy bokeh background required. 【书怪小怪｜祖尔法拉克（Zul'Farrak）】水元素（Water Elemental）。魔兽世界地下城设定下的单体角色立绘或小场景胸像，方图构图、主体居中、剪影在缩略图尺度可读。 背景为高度虚化的统一冷灰 bokeh（石板灰 #94a3a8 系），低饱和、边缘略压暗炭灰 #475569，无职业色光晕、无整块抢镜彩色氛围。 Heavily blurred bokeh background dominated by unified cool neutral gray (#94a3a8, slate), low saturation, slightly darker charcoal #475569 at edges, no colored class glow. 饥荒（Don't Starve）/ Klei 手绘感：墨线勾边、线宽略抖、低饱和大地色系、平涂或轻排线、木偶感比例、阴郁怪趣味。 Klei Don't Starve style: hand-ink outlines, slightly jittery line weight, flat or lightly hatched fills, desaturated earthy palette, puppet-like stylized proportions, subtle grim whimsy. NOT photoreal, NOT glossy anime cel, NOT soft airbrush beauty, NOT clean Pixar 3D. 主体设色：角色与装备用色鲜艳醒目、饱和度高，明暗与色块对比强烈、轮廓与色块交界利落；与虚化低饱和背景形成清晰层次分离，缩略图一眼可读。勿把全身涂成灰褐糊成一团。 Subject coloring: vivid saturated hues on character and gear, strong value/chroma contrast, crisp shapes; clear figure/ground separation from soft desaturated bokeh. Must read as a colorful silhouette at thumbnail size.  外观与设定要点：由清澈海水构成的人形元素生物 祖尔法拉克中的古老元素 水流冲击：造成伤害并减速 World of Warcraft fantasy creature, readable silhouette at thumbnail size, inked rim light not soft bloom. ### 最终首领 — 提示词
```

- **首领**：水术师维尔的拉萨（Hydromancer Velratha）
- **类型**：关卡首领
- **bossUid**：`B000058`
- **表 id**：`boss_ch58_hydromancer_velratha`

```text
【关卡首领】水术师维尔的拉萨（Hydromancer Velratha）。地下城：祖尔法拉克 / Zul'Farrak。关卡语境：祖尔法拉克-第一关。首领需要更强剪影与略大魄力，仍为饥荒手绘线稿风而非写实 Boss 海报。 背景为高度虚化的统一暗红与酒红 bokeh（#450a0a、#7f1d1d 系），阴郁低饱和、边缘略发黑，避免亮橙火焰铺满。 Heavily blurred bokeh background dominated by unified dark crimson and burgundy (#450a0a, #7f1d1d), ominous low saturation, slightly blackened edges, no bright orange flames. 【首领立绘硬性要求】背景必须是暗红/酒红虚化 bokeh，禁止冷灰、石板灰、蓝灰 bokeh；勿与小怪共用灰色背景。 MANDATORY for dungeon boss portrait: background MUST be dark crimson/burgundy bokeh only; NOT cool gray, slate, or blue-gray bokeh; NOT the same neutral gray as trash mobs. 饥荒（Don't Starve）/ Klei 手绘感：墨线勾边、线宽略抖、低饱和大地色系、平涂或轻排线、木偶感比例、阴郁怪趣味。 Klei Don't Starve style: hand-ink outlines, slightly jittery line weight, flat or lightly hatched fills, desaturated earthy palette, puppet-like stylized proportions, subtle grim whimsy. NOT photoreal, NOT glossy anime cel, NOT soft airbrush beauty, NOT clean Pixar 3D. 主体设色：角色与装备用色鲜艳醒目、饱和度高，明暗与色块对比强烈、轮廓与色块交界利落；与虚化低饱和背景形成清晰层次分离，缩略图一眼可读。勿把全身涂成灰褐糊成一团。 Subject coloring: vivid saturated hues on character and gear, strong value/chroma contrast, crisp shapes; clear figure/ground separation from soft desaturated bokeh. Must read as a colorful silhouette at thumbnail size.  设定要点：娜迦水系法师，身披蓝色鳞甲，手持珊瑚权杖 水流冲击：造成伤害并减速；治疗之泉：创造治疗泉水；水牢：困住单个敌人 World of Warcraft dungeon boss portrait, dramatic puppet-like stylization, dark red burgundy bokeh background required. Avoid: circular badge UI frame, watermark, readable text, photoreal skin, glossy anime highlights, Octane 3D, busy sharp readable full dungeon map as background, gore. 设定标签（勿在画面写文字）：远程，生物，辅助
```

NOT photoreal, NOT glossy anime cel, NOT soft airbrush beauty, NOT clean Pixar 3D. 主体设色：角色与装备用色鲜艳醒目、饱和度高，明暗与色块对比强烈、轮廓与色块交界利落；与虚化低饱和背景形成清晰层次分离，缩略图一眼可读。勿把全身涂成灰褐糊成一团。 Subject coloring: vivid saturated hues on character and gear, strong value/chroma contrast, crisp shapes; clear figure/ground separation from soft desaturated bokeh. Must read as a colorful silhouette at thumbnail size.  设定要点：巨魔亡灵战士，身披破烂战甲，手持生锈的武器 暗影斩击：用幽灵武器劈砍；灵魂护盾：吸收伤害；虚弱打击：降低敌人攻击力 World of Warcraft dungeon boss portrait, dramatic puppet-like stylization, dark red burgundy bokeh background required. Avoid: circular badge UI frame, watermark, readable text, photoreal skin, glossy anime highlights, Octane 3D, busy sharp readable full dungeon map as background, gore. 设定标签（勿在画面写文字）：近战，亡灵，输出

### 最终首领 — 提示词

- **首领**：诺克希恩（Noxxion）
- **类型**：关卡首领
- **bossUid**：`B000066`
- **表 id**：`boss_ch66_noxxion`

```text
【关卡首领】诺克希恩（Noxxion）。地下城：玛拉顿 / Maraudon。关卡语境：玛拉顿-第一关。首领需要更强剪影与略大魄力，仍为饥荒手绘线稿风而非写实 Boss 海报。 背景为高度虚化的统一暗红与酒红 bokeh（#450a0a、#7f1d1d 系），阴郁低饱和、边缘略发黑，避免亮橙火焰铺满。 Heavily blurred bokeh background dominated by unified dark crimson and burgundy (#450a0a, #7f1d1d), ominous low saturation, slightly blackened edges, no bright orange flames. 【首领立绘硬性要求】背景必须是暗红/酒红虚化 bokeh，禁止冷灰、石板灰、蓝灰 bokeh；勿与小怪共用灰色背景。 MANDATORY for dungeon boss portrait: background MUST be dark crimson/burgundy bokeh only; NOT cool gray, slate, or blue-gray bokeh; NOT the same neutral gray as trash mobs. 饥荒（Don't Starve）/ Klei 手绘感：墨线勾边、线宽略抖、低饱和大地色系、平涂或轻排线、木偶感比例、阴郁怪趣味。 Klei Don't Starve style: hand-ink outlines, slightly jittery line weight, flat or lightly hatched fills, desaturated earthy palette, puppet-like stylized proportions, subtle grim whimsy. NOT photoreal, NOT glossy anime cel, NOT soft airbrush beauty, NOT clean Pixar 3D. 主体设色：角色与装备用色鲜艳醒目、饱和度高，明暗与色块对比强烈、轮廓与色块交界利落；与虚化低饱和背景形成清晰层次分离，缩略图一眼可读。勿把全身涂成灰褐糊成一团。 Subject coloring: vivid saturated hues on character and gear, strong value/chroma contrast, crisp shapes; clear figure/ground separation from soft desaturated bokeh. Must read as a colorful silhouette at thumbnail size.  设定要点：由腐化能量构成的元素生物，身体呈深紫色，散发着有毒蒸气 酸液池：在脚下创造酸液池；毒液喷射：造成范围自然伤害；分裂：分裂成多个小型本体 World of Warcraft dungeon boss portrait, dramatic puppet-like stylization, dark red burgundy bokeh background required. Avoid: circular badge UI frame, watermark, readable text, photoreal skin, glossy anime highlights, Octane 3D, busy sharp readable full dungeon map as background, gore. 设定标签（勿在画面写文字）：近战，元素，输出
```

NOT photoreal, NOT glossy anime cel, NOT soft airbrush beauty, NOT clean Pixar 3D. 主体设色：角色与装备用色鲜艳醒目、饱和度高，明暗与色块对比强烈、轮廓与色块交界利落；与虚化低饱和背景形成清晰层次分离，缩略图一眼可读。勿把全身涂成灰褐糊成一团。 Subject coloring: vivid saturated hues on character and gear, strong value/chroma contrast, crisp shapes; clear figure/ground separation from soft desaturated bokeh. Must read as a colorful silhouette at thumbnail size.  设定要点：巨大的山岭巨人，身体由岩石构成 震地：踩踏造成范围伤害；石拳：用巨大的拳头攻击；召唤石灵：召唤石灵协助战斗 World of Warcraft dungeon boss portrait, dramatic puppet-like stylization, dark red burgundy bokeh background required. Avoid: circular badge UI frame, watermark, readable text, photoreal skin, glossy anime highlights, Octane 3D, busy sharp readable full dungeon map as background, gore. 设定标签（勿在画面写文字）：近战，元素，坦克

### 最终首领 — 提示词

- **首领**：哈卡尔的化身（Avatar of Hakkar）
- **类型**：关卡首领
- **bossUid**：`B000074`
- **表 id**：`boss_ch74_avatar_of_hakkar`

```text
【关卡首领】哈卡尔的化身（Avatar of Hakkar）。地下城：沉没的神庙 / Sunken Temple。关卡语境：沉没的神庙-第一关。首领需要更强剪影与略大魄力，仍为饥荒手绘线稿风而非写实 Boss 海报。 背景为高度虚化的统一暗红与酒红 bokeh（#450a0a、#7f1d1d 系），阴郁低饱和、边缘略发黑，避免亮橙火焰铺满。 Heavily blurred bokeh background dominated by unified dark crimson and burgundy (#450a0a, #7f1d1d), ominous low saturation, slightly blackened edges, no bright orange flames. 【首领立绘硬性要求】背景必须是暗红/酒红虚化 bokeh，禁止冷灰、石板灰、蓝灰 bokeh；勿与小怪共用灰色背景。 MANDATORY for dungeon boss portrait: background MUST be dark crimson/burgundy bokeh only; NOT cool gray, slate, or blue-gray bokeh; NOT the same neutral gray as trash mobs. 饥荒（Don't Starve）/ Klei 手绘感：墨线勾边、线宽略抖、低饱和大地色系、平涂或轻排线、木偶感比例、阴郁怪趣味。 Klei Don't Starve style: hand-ink outlines, slightly jittery line weight, flat or lightly hatched fills, desaturated earthy palette, puppet-like stylized proportions, subtle grim whimsy. Must read as a colorful silhouette at thumbnail size.  设定要点：巨大的灵魂生物，由橙红色火焰构成 灵魂冲击：穿透敌人造成伤害；炽热光环：周围持续受到火焰伤害；灵魂锁链：束缚敌人 World of Warcraft dungeon boss portrait, dramatic puppet-like stylization, dark red burgundy bokeh background required. ### 最终首领 — 提示词
```

- **首领**：贝恩加（Bael'gar）
- **类型**：关卡首领
- **bossUid**：`B000078`
- **表 id**：`boss_ch78_bael_gar`

```text
【关卡首领】贝恩加（Bael'gar）。地下城：黑石深渊 / Blackrock Depths。关卡语境：黑石深渊-第一关。首领需要更强剪影与略大魄力，仍为饥荒手绘线稿风而非写实 Boss 海报。 背景为高度虚化的统一暗红与酒红 bokeh（#450a0a、#7f1d1d 系），阴郁低饱和、边缘略发黑，避免亮橙火焰铺满。 Heavily blurred bokeh background dominated by unified dark crimson and burgundy (#450a0a, #7f1d1d), ominous low saturation, slightly blackened edges, no bright orange flames. 【首领立绘硬性要求】背景必须是暗红/酒红虚化 bokeh，禁止冷灰、石板灰、蓝灰 bokeh；勿与小怪共用灰色背景。 MANDATORY for dungeon boss portrait: background MUST be dark crimson/burgundy bokeh only; NOT cool gray, slate, or blue-gray bokeh; NOT the same neutral gray as trash mobs. 饥荒（Don't Starve）/ Klei 手绘感：墨线勾边、线宽略抖、低饱和大地色系、平涂或轻排线、木偶感比例、阴郁怪趣味。 Klei Don't Starve style: hand-ink outlines, slightly jittery line weight, flat or lightly hatched fills, desaturated earthy palette, puppet-like stylized proportions, subtle grim whimsy. NOT photoreal, NOT glossy anime cel, NOT soft airbrush beauty, NOT clean Pixar 3D. 主体设色：角色与装备用色鲜艳醒目、饱和度高，明暗与色块对比强烈、轮廓与色块交界利落；与虚化低饱和背景形成清晰层次分离，缩略图一眼可读。勿把全身涂成灰褐糊成一团。 Subject coloring: vivid saturated hues on character and gear, strong value/chroma contrast, crisp shapes; clear figure/ground separation from soft desaturated bokeh. Must read as a colorful silhouette at thumbnail size.  设定要点：火焰巨灵，身体由熔岩构成 熔岩拳：用熔岩拳头攻击；火焰爆发：从身体爆发火焰；炽热光环：周围持续受到火焰伤害 World of Warcraft dungeon boss portrait, dramatic puppet-like stylization, dark red burgundy bokeh background required. Avoid: circular badge UI frame, watermark, readable text, photoreal skin, glossy anime highlights, Octane 3D, busy sharp readable full dungeon map as background, gore. 设定标签（勿在画面写文字）：近战，元素，坦克
```

```text

【关卡首领】麦姆·格洛格（Magmus）。地下城：黑石深渊 / Blackrock Depths。关卡语境：黑石深渊-第十一关。首领需要更强剪影与略大魄力，仍为饥荒手绘线稿风而非写实 Boss 海报。 背景为高度虚化的统一暗红与酒红 bokeh（#450a0a、#7f1d1d 系），阴郁低饱和、边缘略发黑，避免亮橙火焰铺满。 Heavily blurred bokeh background dominated by unified dark crimson and burgundy (#450a0a, #7f1d1d), ominous low saturation, slightly blackened edges, no bright orange flames. 【首领立绘硬性要求】背景必须是暗红/酒红虚化 bokeh，禁止冷灰、石板灰、蓝灰 bokeh；勿与小怪共用灰色背景。 MANDATORY for dungeon boss portrait: background MUST be dark crimson/burgundy bokeh only; NOT cool gray, slate, or blue-gray bokeh; NOT the same neutral gray as trash mobs. 饥荒（Don't Starve）/ Klei 手绘感：墨线勾边、线宽略抖、低饱和大地色系、平涂或轻排线、木偶感比例、阴郁怪趣味。 Klei Don't Starve style: hand-ink outlines, slightly jittery line weight, flat or lightly hatched fills, desaturated earthy palette, puppet-like stylized proportions, subtle grim whimsy. NOT photoreal, NOT glossy anime cel, NOT soft airbrush beauty, NOT clean Pixar 3D. 主体设色：角色与装备用色鲜艳醒目、饱和度高，明暗与色块对比强烈、轮廓与色块交界利落；与虚化低饱和背景形成清晰层次分离，缩略图一眼可读。勿把全身涂成灰褐糊成一团。 Subject coloring: vivid saturated hues on character and gear, strong value/chroma contrast, crisp shapes; clear figure/ground separation from soft desaturated bokeh. Must read as a colorful silhouette at thumbnail size.  设定要点：火焰巨人 熔岩拳：用熔岩拳头攻击；火焰爆发：从身体爆发火焰；炽热光环：周围持续受到火焰伤害 World of Warcraft dungeon boss portrait, dramatic puppet-like stylization, dark red burgundy bokeh background required. Avoid: circular badge UI frame, watermark, readable text, photoreal skin, glossy anime highlights, Octane 3D, busy sharp readable full dungeon map as background, gore. 设定标签（勿在画面写文字）：近战，元素，坦克
```

```text
【书怪小怪｜厄运之槌（Dire Maul）】水元素（Hydrospawn Minion）。魔兽世界地下城设定下的单体角色立绘或小场景胸像，方图构图、主体居中、剪影在缩略图尺度可读。 背景为高度虚化的统一冷灰 bokeh（石板灰 #94a3a8 系），低饱和、边缘略压暗炭灰 #475569，无职业色光晕、无整块抢镜彩色氛围。 Heavily blurred bokeh background dominated by unified cool neutral gray (#94a3a8, slate), low saturation, slightly darker charcoal #475569 at edges, no colored class glow. 饥荒（Don't Starve）/ Klei 手绘感：墨线勾边、线宽略抖、低饱和大地色系、平涂或轻排线、木偶感比例、阴郁怪趣味。 Klei Don't Starve style: hand-ink outlines, slightly jittery line weight, flat or lightly hatched fills, desaturated earthy palette, puppet-like stylized proportions, subtle grim whimsy. NOT photoreal, NOT glossy anime cel, NOT soft airbrush beauty, NOT clean Pixar 3D. 主体设色：角色与装备用色鲜艳醒目、饱和度高，明暗与色块对比强烈、轮廓与色块交界利落；与虚化低饱和背景形成清晰层次分离，缩略图一眼可读。勿把全身涂成灰褐糊成一团。 Subject coloring: vivid saturated hues on character and gear, strong value/chroma contrast, crisp shapes; clear figure/ground separation from soft desaturated bokeh. Must read as a colorful silhouette at thumbnail size.  外观与设定要点：水元素的小型版本 是 是 World of Warcraft fantasy creature, readable silhouette at thumbnail size, inked rim light not soft bloom. Avoid: circular badge UI frame, watermark, readable text, photoreal skin, glossy anime highlights, Octane 3D, busy sharp readable full dungeon map as background, gore. 设定标签（勿在画面写文字）：近战，元素，输出
```

```text
【关卡首领】普斯林（Pusillin）。地下城：厄运之槌 / Dire Maul。关卡语境：厄运之槌-第一关。首领需要更强剪影与略大魄力，仍为饥荒手绘线稿风而非写实 Boss 海报。 背景为高度虚化的统一暗红与酒红 bokeh（#450a0a、#7f1d1d 系），阴郁低饱和、边缘略发黑，避免亮橙火焰铺满。 Heavily blurred bokeh background dominated by unified dark crimson and burgundy (#450a0a, #7f1d1d), ominous low saturation, slightly blackened edges, no bright orange flames. 【首领立绘硬性要求】背景必须是暗红/酒红虚化 bokeh，禁止冷灰、石板灰、蓝灰 bokeh；勿与小怪共用灰色背景。 MANDATORY for dungeon boss portrait: background MUST be dark crimson/burgundy bokeh only; NOT cool gray, slate, or blue-gray bokeh; NOT the same neutral gray as trash mobs. 饥荒（Don't Starve）/ Klei 手绘感：墨线勾边、线宽略抖、低饱和大地色系、平涂或轻排线、木偶感比例、阴郁怪趣味。 Klei Don't Starve style: hand-ink outlines, slightly jittery line weight, flat or lightly hatched fills, desaturated earthy palette, puppet-like stylized proportions, subtle grim whimsy. NOT photoreal, NOT glossy anime cel, NOT soft airbrush beauty, NOT clean Pixar 3D. 主体设色：角色与装备用色鲜艳醒目、饱和度高，明暗与色块对比强烈、轮廓与色块交界利落；与虚化低饱和背景形成清晰层次分离，缩略图一眼可读。勿把全身涂成灰褐糊成一团。 Subject coloring: vivid saturated hues on character and gear, strong value/chroma contrast, crisp shapes; clear figure/ground separation from soft desaturated bokeh. Must read as a colorful silhouette at thumbnail size.  设定要点：小鬼形态的恶作剧者 暗影弹：发射暗影能量；闪烁：瞬移；召唤：召唤小鬼协助 World of Warcraft dungeon boss portrait, dramatic puppet-like stylization, dark red burgundy bokeh background required. ### 最终首领 — 提示词
```

- **首领**：不可宽恕者（The Unforgiven）
- **类型**：关卡首领
- **bossUid**：`B000095`
- **表 id**：`boss_ch95_the_unforgiven`

```text
【关卡首领】不可宽恕者（The Unforgiven）。地下城：斯坦索姆 / Stratholme。关卡语境：斯坦索姆-第一关。首领需要更强剪影与略大魄力，仍为饥荒手绘线稿风而非写实 Boss 海报。 背景为高度虚化的统一暗红与酒红 bokeh（#450a0a、#7f1d1d 系），阴郁低饱和、边缘略发黑，避免亮橙火焰铺满。 Heavily blurred bokeh background dominated by unified dark crimson and burgundy (#450a0a, #7f1d1d), ominous low saturation, slightly blackened edges, no bright orange flames. 【首领立绘硬性要求】背景必须是暗红/酒红虚化 bokeh，禁止冷灰、石板灰、蓝灰 bokeh；勿与小怪共用灰色背景。 MANDATORY for dungeon boss portrait: background MUST be dark crimson/burgundy bokeh only; NOT cool gray, slate, or blue-gray bokeh; NOT the same neutral gray as trash mobs. 饥荒（Don't Starve）/ Klei 手绘感：墨线勾边、线宽略抖、低饱和大地色系、平涂或轻排线、木偶感比例、阴郁怪趣味。 Klei Don't Starve style: hand-ink outlines, slightly jittery line weight, flat or lightly hatched fills, desaturated earthy palette, puppet-like stylized proportions, subtle grim whimsy. NOT photoreal, NOT glossy anime cel, NOT soft airbrush beauty, NOT clean Pixar 3D. 主体设色：角色与装备用色鲜艳醒目、饱和度高，明暗与色块对比强烈、轮廓与色块交界利落；与虚化低饱和背景形成清晰层次分离，缩略图一眼可读。勿把全身涂成灰褐糊成一团。 Subject coloring: vivid saturated hues on character and gear, strong value/chroma contrast, crisp shapes; clear figure/ground separation from soft desaturated bokeh. Must read as a colorful silhouette at thumbnail size.  设定要点：亡灵战士 顺劈斩：攻击面前所有敌人；暗影打击：造成暗影伤害；亡灵护甲：受到伤害减免 World of Warcraft dungeon boss portrait, dramatic puppet-like stylization, dark red burgundy bokeh background required. Avoid: circular badge UI frame, watermark, readable text, photoreal skin, glossy anime highlights, Octane 3D, busy sharp readable full dungeon map as background, gore. 设定标签（勿在画面写文字）：近战，亡灵，坦克
```

```text
【关卡首领】残忍的蒂米（Timmy the Cruel）。地下城：斯坦索姆 / Stratholme。关卡语境：斯坦索姆-第三关。首领需要更强剪影与略大魄力，仍为饥荒手绘线稿风而非写实 Boss 海报。 背景为高度虚化的统一暗红与酒红 bokeh（#450a0a、#7f1d1d 系），阴郁低饱和、边缘略发黑，避免亮橙火焰铺满。 Heavily blurred bokeh background dominated by unified dark crimson and burgundy (#450a0a, #7f1d1d), ominous low saturation, slightly blackened edges, no bright orange flames. 【首领立绘硬性要求】背景必须是暗红/酒红虚化 bokeh，禁止冷灰、石板灰、蓝灰 bokeh；勿与小怪共用灰色背景。 MANDATORY for dungeon boss portrait: background MUST be dark crimson/burgundy bokeh only; NOT cool gray, slate, or blue-gray bokeh; NOT the same neutral gray as trash mobs. 饥荒（Don't Starve）/ Klei 手绘感：墨线勾边、线宽略抖、低饱和大地色系、平涂或轻排线、木偶感比例、阴郁怪趣味。 Klei Don't Starve style: hand-ink outlines, slightly jittery line weight, flat or lightly hatched fills, desaturated earthy palette, puppet-like stylized proportions, subtle grim whimsy. NOT photoreal, NOT glossy anime cel, NOT soft airbrush beauty, NOT clean Pixar 3D. 主体设色：角色与装备用色鲜艳醒目、饱和度高，明暗与色块对比强烈、轮廓与色块交界利落；与虚化低饱和背景形成清晰层次分离，缩略图一眼可读。勿把全身涂成灰褐糊成一团。 Subject coloring: vivid saturated hues on character and gear, strong value/chroma contrast, crisp shapes; clear figure/ground separation from soft desaturated bokeh. Must read as a colorful silhouette at thumbnail size.  设定要点：疯狂的亡灵小鬼 撕咬：用利爪撕咬；狂暴：提升攻击速度；恐惧：使敌人逃跑 World of Warcraft dungeon boss portrait, dramatic puppet-like stylization, dark red burgundy bokeh background required. Avoid: circular badge UI frame, watermark, readable text, photoreal skin, glossy anime highlights, Octane 3D, busy sharp readable full dungeon map as background, gore. 设定标签（勿在画面写文字）：近战，亡灵，输出
```

### 最终首领 — 提示词

- **首领**：严寒导师（Instructor Chillheart）
- **类型**：关卡首领
- **bossUid**：`B000102`
- **表 id**：`boss_ch102_instructor_chillheart`

```text
【关卡首领】严寒导师（Instructor Chillheart）。地下城：通灵学院 / Scholomance。关卡语境：通灵学院-第一关。首领需要更强剪影与略大魄力，仍为饥荒手绘线稿风而非写实 Boss 海报。 背景为高度虚化的统一暗红与酒红 bokeh（#450a0a、#7f1d1d 系），阴郁低饱和、边缘略发黑，避免亮橙火焰铺满。 Heavily blurred bokeh background dominated by unified dark crimson and burgundy (#450a0a, #7f1d1d), ominous low saturation, slightly blackened edges, no bright orange flames. 【首领立绘硬性要求】背景必须是暗红/酒红虚化 bokeh，禁止冷灰、石板灰、蓝灰 bokeh；勿与小怪共用灰色背景。 MANDATORY for dungeon boss portrait: background MUST be dark crimson/burgundy bokeh only; NOT cool gray, slate, or blue-gray bokeh; NOT the same neutral gray as trash mobs. 饥荒（Don't Starve）/ Klei 手绘感：墨线勾边、线宽略抖、低饱和大地色系、平涂或轻排线、木偶感比例、阴郁怪趣味。 Klei Don't Starve style: hand-ink outlines, slightly jittery line weight, flat or lightly hatched fills, desaturated earthy palette, puppet-like stylized proportions, subtle grim whimsy. NOT photoreal, NOT glossy anime cel, NOT soft airbrush beauty, NOT clean Pixar 3D. 主体设色：角色与装备用色鲜艳醒目、饱和度高，明暗与色块对比强烈、轮廓与色块交界利落；与虚化低饱和背景形成清晰层次分离，缩略图一眼可读。勿把全身涂成灰褐糊成一团。 Subject coloring: vivid saturated hues on character and gear, strong value/chroma contrast, crisp shapes; clear figure/ground separation from soft desaturated bokeh. Must read as a colorful silhouette at thumbnail size.  设定要点：冰冷的亡灵法师 寒冰箭：发射冰霜箭矢；寒冰新星：冻结周围敌人；寒冰之墓：将敌人冻结在冰中 World of Warcraft dungeon boss portrait, dramatic puppet-like stylization, dark red burgundy bokeh background required. Avoid: circular badge UI frame, watermark, readable text, photoreal skin, glossy anime highlights, Octane 3D, busy sharp readable full dungeon map as background, gore. 设定标签（勿在画面写文字）：远程，亡灵，输出
```

NOT photoreal, NOT glossy anime cel, NOT soft airbrush beauty, NOT clean Pixar 3D. 主体设色：角色与装备用色鲜艳醒目、饱和度高，明暗与色块对比强烈、轮廓与色块交界利落；与虚化低饱和背景形成清晰层次分离，缩略图一眼可读。勿把全身涂成灰褐糊成一团。 Subject coloring: vivid saturated hues on character and gear, strong value/chroma contrast, crisp shapes; clear figure/ground separation from soft desaturated bokeh. Must read as a colorful silhouette at thumbnail size.  设定要点：堕落的圣骑士 制裁之锤：造成神圣伤害并眩晕；神圣之火：造成神圣伤害；命令：提升友军攻击力 World of Warcraft dungeon boss portrait, dramatic puppet-like stylization, dark red burgundy bokeh background required. Avoid: circular badge UI frame, watermark, readable text, photoreal skin, glossy anime highlights, Octane 3D, busy sharp readable full dungeon map as background, gore. 设定标签（勿在画面写文字）：近战，亡灵，输出

### 最终首领 — 提示词

- **首领**：奥莫克将军（Highlord Omokk）
- **类型**：关卡首领
- **bossUid**：`B000107`
- **表 id**：`boss_ch107_highlord_omokk`

```text
【关卡首领】奥莫克将军（Highlord Omokk）。地下城：黑石塔下层 / Lower Blackrock Spire。关卡语境：黑石塔下层-第一关。首领需要更强剪影与略大魄力，仍为饥荒手绘线稿风而非写实 Boss 海报。 背景为高度虚化的统一暗红与酒红 bokeh（#450a0a、#7f1d1d 系），阴郁低饱和、边缘略发黑，避免亮橙火焰铺满。 Heavily blurred bokeh background dominated by unified dark crimson and burgundy (#450a0a, #7f1d1d), ominous low saturation, slightly blackened edges, no bright orange flames. 【首领立绘硬性要求】背景必须是暗红/酒红虚化 bokeh，禁止冷灰、石板灰、蓝灰 bokeh；勿与小怪共用灰色背景。 MANDATORY for dungeon boss portrait: background MUST be dark crimson/burgundy bokeh only; NOT cool gray, slate, or blue-gray bokeh; NOT the same neutral gray as trash mobs. 饥荒（Don't Starve）/ Klei 手绘感：墨线勾边、线宽略抖、低饱和大地色系、平涂或轻排线、木偶感比例、阴郁怪趣味。 Klei Don't Starve style: hand-ink outlines, slightly jittery line weight, flat or lightly hatched fills, desaturated earthy palette, puppet-like stylized proportions, subtle grim whimsy. NOT photoreal, NOT glossy anime cel, NOT soft airbrush beauty, NOT clean Pixar 3D. 主体设色：角色与装备用色鲜艳醒目、饱和度高，明暗与色块对比强烈、轮廓与色块交界利落；与虚化低饱和背景形成清晰层次分离，缩略图一眼可读。勿把全身涂成灰褐糊成一团。 Subject coloring: vivid saturated hues on character and gear, strong value/chroma contrast, crisp shapes; clear figure/ground separation from soft desaturated bokeh. Must read as a colorful silhouette at thumbnail size.  设定要点：黑石兽人首领 顺劈斩：攻击面前多个敌人；冲锋：高速冲向敌人；狂暴：提升攻击力 World of Warcraft dungeon boss portrait, dramatic puppet-like stylization, dark red burgundy bokeh background required. NOT photoreal, NOT glossy anime cel, NOT soft airbrush beauty, NOT clean Pixar 3D. 主体设色：角色与装备用色鲜艳醒目、饱和度高，明暗与色块对比强烈、轮廓与色块交界利落；与虚化低饱和背景形成清晰层次分离，缩略图一眼可读。勿把全身涂成灰褐糊成一团。 Subject coloring: vivid saturated hues on character and gear, strong value/chroma contrast, crisp shapes; clear figure/ground separation from soft desaturated bokeh. Must read as a colorful silhouette at thumbnail size.  设定要点：黑铁矮人军需官 顺劈斩：攻击面前多个敌人；战斗怒吼：提升友军攻击力；盾击：用盾牌击晕 World of Warcraft dungeon boss portrait, dramatic puppet-like stylization, dark red burgundy bokeh background required. Avoid: circular badge UI frame, watermark, readable text, photoreal skin, glossy anime highlights, Octane 3D, busy sharp readable full dungeon map as background, gore. 设定标签（勿在画面写文字）：近战，生物，坦克
```
